
For 4.14.216:
CONFIG_CRYPTO_MANAGER_EXTRA_TESTS Enable extra run-time crypto self tests does not exist.

For 5.4.90:
CONFIG_CRYPTO_MANAGER_EXTRA_TESTS Enable extra run-time crypto self tests was enabled.

For 5.10.8:
CONFIG_CRYPTO_MANAGER_EXTRA_TESTS Enable extra run-time crypto self tests was disabled.
